    互联网架构，如何进行容量设计？

    架构 架构
    创建时间:2016-08-25 11:44

    ##
    一，需求缘起

    <span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">互联网公司，这样的场景是否似曾相识：</span>

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">场景一：</span>pm<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">要做一个很大的运营活动，技术老大杀过来，问了两个问题：</span>

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">（</span>1<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">）<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">机器能抗住么？</span></span>

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">（</span>2<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">）<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">如果扛不住，需要加多少台机器？</span></span>

&nbsp;

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">场景二：系统设计阶段，技术老大杀过来，又问了两个问题：</span>

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">（</span>1<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">）<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">数据库需要分库么？</span></span>

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">（</span>2<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">）<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">如果需要分库，需要分几个库？</span></span>

&nbsp;

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">技术上来说，这些都是系统容量预估的问题，**容量设计是架构师必备的技能之一**。常见的容量评估包括数据量、并发量、带宽、</span>CPU/MEM/DISK<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">等，今天分享的内容，就<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">以【并发量】为例</span>，看看如何回答好这两个问题。</span>

&nbsp;

    ##
    二，容量评估的步骤与方法

    **<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">【步骤一：评估总访问量】</span>**

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">如何知道总访问量？</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">对于一个运营活动的访问量评估，或者一个系统上线后</span>PV<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">的评估，有什么好的方法？</span>

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">答案是：询问业务方</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">，询问运营同学，询问产品同学，看对运营活动或者产品上线后的预期是什么。</span>

&nbsp;

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">举例：</span>58<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">要做一个</span>APP-push<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">的运营活动，计划在</span>30<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">分钟内完成</span>5000w<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">用户的</span>push<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">推送，预计</span>push<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">消息点击率</span>10%<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">，求</span>push<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">落地页系统的总访问量？</span>

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">回答：</span>5000w*10% = 500w

&nbsp;

**<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">【步骤二：评估平均访问量</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">】</span>**

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">如何知道平均访问量</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">？</span></span>

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">答案是：有了总量，除以总时间</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">即可，如果按照天评估，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">一天按照</span>4w<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">秒计算</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">。</span>

&nbsp;

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">举例</span>1<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">：</span>push<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">落地页系统</span>30<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">分钟的总访问量是</span>500w<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">，求平均访问量</span>QPS

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">回答：</span>500w/(30*60) = 2778<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">，大概</span>3000QPS

&nbsp;

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">举例</span>2<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">：主站首页估计日均</span>pv 8000w<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">，求平均访问</span>QPS

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">回答：一天按照</span>4w<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">秒算，</span>8000w/4w=2000<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">，大概</span>2000QPS

&nbsp;

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">提问：为什么一天按照</span>4w<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">秒计算？</span></span>

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">回答：一天共</span>24<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">小时</span>*60<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">分钟</span>*60<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">秒</span>=8w<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">秒，<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">一般假设所有请求都发生在白天</span>，所以一般来说一天只按照</span>4w<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">秒评估</span>

&nbsp;

**<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">【步骤三：评估高峰</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">】</span>**

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">系统容量规划时，不能只考虑平均</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">，而是要抗住高峰的</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">如何知道高峰</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">呢？</span></span>

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">答案是：<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">根据业务特性，通过业务访问曲线评估</span></span>

&nbsp;

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">举例：日均</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">为</span>2000<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">，业务访问趋势图如下图，求峰值</span>QPS预估<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">？</span>

&nbsp;

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">说明：有一些业务例如&ldquo;秒杀业务&rdquo;比较难画出业务访问趋势图，这类业务的容量评估不在此列。</span>

&nbsp;

**<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">【步骤四：评估系统、单机极限</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">】</span>**

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">如何评估一个业务，一个服务单机能的极限</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">呢？</span></span>

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">答案是：压力测试</span>

&nbsp;

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">在一个服务上线前，一般来说是需要进行压力测试的（很多创业型公司，业务迭代很快的系统可能没有这一步，那就悲剧了），以</span>APP-push<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">运营活动落地页为例（日均</span>QPS2000<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">，峰值</span>QPS5000<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">），这个系统的架构可能是这样的：</span>

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; line-height: 1.6; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">1</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; line-height: 1.6; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">）访问端是</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; line-height: 1.6; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">APP</span>

2<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">）运营活动</span>H5<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">落地页是一个</span>web<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">站点</span>

3<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">）</span>H5<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">落地页由缓存</span>cache<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">、数据库</span>db<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">中的数据拼装而成</span>

&nbsp;

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">通过压力测试发现，</span>web<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">层是瓶颈，</span>tomcat<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">压测单机只能抗住</span>1200<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">的</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">（一般来说，</span>1%<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">的流量到数据库，数据库</span>500QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">还是能轻松抗住的，</span>cache<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">的话</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">能抗住，需要评估</span>cache<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">的带宽，假设不是瓶颈），我们就得到了</span>web<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">单机极限的</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">是</span>1200<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">。一般来说，线上系统是不会跑满到极限的，打个</span>8<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">折，单机</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">线上允许跑到</span>QPS1000</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">。</span>

&nbsp;

**<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">【步骤五：根据线上冗余度回答两个问题】</span>**

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">好了，上述步骤</span>1-4<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">已经得到了</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">峰值</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">是</span>5000<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">，单机</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">是</span>1000<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">，假设线上部署了</span>2<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">台服务</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">，就能自信自如的回答技术老大提出的问题了：</span>

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">（</span>1<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">）机器能抗住么？</span> -&gt; <span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">峰值</span>5000<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">，单机</span>1000<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">，线上</span>2<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">台，<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">扛不住</span></span>

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">（</span>2<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">）如果扛不住，需要加多少台机器？</span> -&gt; <span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">需要额外</span>3<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">台</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">，提前预留</span>1<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">台更好，给</span>4<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">台更稳</span>

&nbsp;

<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">除了并发量的容量预估，数据量、带宽、</span>CPU/MEM/DISK<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">等评估亦可遵循类似的步骤。</span>

&nbsp;

    ##
    三，总结

    <span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">互联网架构设计如何进行容量评估：</span>

**<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">【步骤一：评估总访问量】</span>** -&gt; <span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">询问业务、产品、运营</span>

**<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">【步骤二：评估平均访问量</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">】</span>**-&gt; <span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">除以时间，一天算</span>4w<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">秒</span></span>

**<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">【步骤三：评估高峰</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">】</span>** -&gt; <span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">根据业务曲线图来</span>

**<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">【步骤四：评估系统、单机极限</span>QPS<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">】</span>** -&gt; <span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">压测很重要</span>

**<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">【步骤五：根据线上冗余度回答两个问题】</span>** -&gt; <span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 76, 0); font-family: 宋体; -ms-word-wrap: break-word !important; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important;">估计冗余度与线上冗余度差值</span>
